[30;1m23 | [0m[35m``NoControlCharactersValidator``[0m
[30;1m24 | [0m[35m~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[0m
[30;1m25 | [0m[35mValidates that Control Characters like new lines or tabs are not allowed.[0m
[30;1m26 | [0m[35mCan optionally specify `whitelist` of control characters to allow.[0m
